<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wind</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherm.html>scherm</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">screen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “windscreen of an aircraft” derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">windscreen</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>A windbreak <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">screen to protect against the wind</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The windscreen of an aircraft.</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the casks stowed in the wings of a vessel's hold, being <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> than such as are stowed more amidships.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> hauled out a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:grog.html>grog</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An offensive player who plays on either side of the center.
<dl><dd><i>The center passed to the left <b><a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a></b>, who shot and scored.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> October 1,  Alistair Magowan,  “Man Utd 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 0 Norwich”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/15045317.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"The pattern of the game could have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> different if Anthony Pilkington <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> one of two chances either side of United's opener.<br />But the Norwich <b><a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a></b> shot wide when clean through and saw another effort hit the post on 75 minutes.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***winkel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a> (1100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corner</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*winkilaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weng-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend, bow, arch, curve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>Winkel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wincel</i>. The meaning "shop" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from the meaning "corner in which merchandise <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> stalled".
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkels.html>winkels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkeltje.html>winkeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>shop (an establishment that sells goods to the public).
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boetiek.html>boetiek</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handel.html>handel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> corner, as in <a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a> (78007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">winkelhake</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">try square, carpenter's square</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haak.html>haak</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Serurista_ortilo.jpg/250px-Serurista_ortilo.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Serurista_ortilo.jpg/375px-Serurista_ortilo.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Serurista_ortilo.jpg/500px-Serurista_ortilo.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1840" data-file-height="840" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>Winkelhaak</a></i><br />Try square</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg/250px-Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="300" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg/375px-Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg/500px-Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg 2x" data-file-width="901" data-file-height="1081" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:textiel.html>textiel</a></i><br />Winkel-hawk in textile</div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>try square; or, generally, any <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of square used by masons and <a href = vnd.unilang:carpenters.html>carpenters</a> to measure right angles, such as a steel square or a carpenter's square</li>
<li>a rectangular tear or cut in a piece of clothing or other fabric, in the form of a try square.</li></ol>

***winnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winnen.html>winnen</a> (686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:winnen.html>winnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">winnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*winnaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wenh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strive, desire, wish, love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winnen.html>winnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to win, to triumph, to be victorious (in)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to acquire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extract, to refine, to harvest (from base materials such as ore or crops)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wirwar.html>wirwar</a> (55393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wirrwarr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wirwar.html>wirwar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wirwar.html>wirwarren</a></b>)
</p>

<p>From earlier Modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wisconst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">art of what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wis.html>wis</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-kunde</i>. Purism introduced by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Stevin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Simon Stevin"><a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Stevin</a> in the 16th century to replace the Dutch word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mathematica</i> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a borrowing from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mathematica</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselen.html>wisselen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselaar.html>wisselaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselaars.html>wisselaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselaar.html>wisselaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">money changer</span></li>
<li>anything that shuffles, changes or exchanges something</li></ol>

***wisselen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wisselen.html>wisselen</a> (4464)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselen.html>wisselen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wissalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihslōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wissel.html>wissel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselen.html>wisselen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swap, to exchange</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to vary, to change (<a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> time, by circumstances etc.)</li></ol>

***wisselgeld.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wisselgeld.html>wisselgeld</a> (5355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wisselgelt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fee for converting to a different currency</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselen.html>wisselen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i>, or less probably <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wissel.html>wissel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselgeld.html>wisselgeld</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>change <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">money returned after not paying exactly; stock of money used for this purpose</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselgeld.html>wisselgeld</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">And then you'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> also get some <b>change</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***wit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> (1863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwittaz</i>. The geminate <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unexpected as the usual <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwītaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱweytos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shine; bright</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The geminate <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes explained as being the result of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kluge%27s_law" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kluge | s law">Kluge's law</a>, thus from a Pre-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kweyd-nos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witter.html>witter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">witst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>white
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wand.html>wand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The (inner) wall <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>white</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Surinam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> having a white skin colour, light-skinned <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see usage note</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Surinam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> having a relatively light skin colour</li>
<li>legal</li>
<li>pure, untainted</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clear-lighted, not dark at all
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewenst.html>gewenste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verscheen.html>verscheen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klaar.html>klaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The long-wished-for day appeared, very clear and <b>white</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Recently, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> come to be used in continental Dutch by some (associated with social justice movements) to refer to a specific skin colour, i.e. to light-skinned people of apparent mostly European descent. Traditionally, the adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> used there for this purpose, and this usage <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> by far the most widespread in the Netherlands and Belgium.
</p>

<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witten.html>witten</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*witją</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge, reason</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see, know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wis.html>wis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Witz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witten.html>witten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>witje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ability to think and reason</li>

***withers.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a> (66523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From dialectal English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wither</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">against</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <i>wither-</i>)  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-s</i>; see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">with</i>. So-named because it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the part of the horse that pushes <i>against</i> a load. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Widerrist</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wider</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">against</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rist</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wrist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>normally plural</i>, <i>singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en">wither</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The part of the back of a four-legged animal that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> between the shoulder <a href = vnd.unilang:blades.html>blades</a>; in many species the highest point of the body and the standard place to measure the animal's height. <span class="defdate">[from 1580]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> in the plural, this noun refers to one object. The synonymous singular, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wither</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> less common.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fistulous <a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wither-wrung</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wring one's <a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Third-person singular simple present indicative form of <span class="mention" lang="en">wither</span></span></li></ol>
</body>

***witt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:witt.html>witt</a> (50228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hwīt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwītaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hvid</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">weiß</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">hvit</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wyt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***woede.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woede.html>woede</a> (2365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wuot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wuodi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wōþuz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wut</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anger, rage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare the related adjective <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wōd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a>, insane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wode</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">insane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woede.html>woede</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>anger, wrath, outrage</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woeden.html>woeden</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woede.html>woede</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention"> singular present subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woeden.html>woeden</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:woede.html>woede</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:woeden.html>woeden</a></i>, a derivate of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woet</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>to rage
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>Onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>Grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:londen.html>Londen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstaat.html>verstaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuurzee.html>vuurzee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanaf.html>vanaf</a> 2 september 1666 (Juliaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:kalender.html>kalender</a>), 12 september 1666 (<a href = vnd.unilang:gregoriaans.html>Gregoriaanse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kalender.html>kalender</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Engelse <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdstad.html>hoofdstad</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:woedde.html>woedde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijk.html>belangrijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwoestte.html>verwoestte</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>  |  By the Great Fire of London one understands the sea of fire which starting on 2 September 1666 (Julian calendar), 12 September 1666 (Gregorian calendar), raged for three days in the English capital and which destroyed an important part of this place.</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:woekeren.html>woekeren</a></i>, derived from the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woekeren.html>woeker</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wuchern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to practise usury; to overgrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> especially of plants</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overgrow

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woensdach</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wuodenesdag</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*Wōdanas dagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day of Woden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a> Mercurii</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woest</a> (5119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:woeste.html>woeste</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wuosti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wōstijaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>(<i>concerning a creature and behavior</i>) wild, savage, feral, ferocious, furious

<dl><dd><i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:rascal.html>rascal</a> often got dad furious</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>concerning a place</i>) inhospitable, rough, wild; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> desolate

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woestijn.html>woestijn</a> (2173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woestine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wuostinna</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wüste</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">waste</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wulfaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wĺ̥kʷos</i>.
</p>
